choose_your_leader_catagory_3 = {


	GER_Adolf_Hitler = {
			
		cost = 0
		days_re_enable = 0
		days_remove = 0
		visible = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CYL_GER
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
		    kill_country_leader = yes
		    if = {
		        limit = {
			        has_government = neutrality
			    }
			    create_country_leader = {
				    name = "Adolf Hitler"
				    picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Adolf_Hitler.dds"
				    expire = "1965.1.1"
				    ideology = despotism
				    traits = {
				    }
			    }
		    }
			if = {
		        limit = {
			        has_government = democratic
			    }
			    create_country_leader = {
				    name = "Adolf Hitler"
				    picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Adolf_Hitler.dds"
				    expire = "1965.1.1"
				    ideology = conservatism
				    traits = {
				    }
			    }
		    }
			if = {
		        limit = {
			        has_government = communism
			    }
			    create_country_leader = {
				    name = "Adolf Hitler"
				    picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Adolf_Hitler.dds"
				    expire = "1965.1.1"
				    ideology = marxism
				    traits = {
				    }
			    }
		    }
			if = {
		        limit = {
			        has_government = fascism
			    }
			    create_country_leader = {
				    name = "Adolf Hitler"
				    picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Adolf_Hitler.dds"
				    expire = "1965.1.1"
				    ideology = fascism_ideology
				    traits = {
				    }
			    }
		    }
	    }

		days_re_enable = 0
		days_remove = 0
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = CYL_ITA
		}
		complete_effect = {
		    kill_country_leader = yes
		    if = {
		        limit = {
			        has_government = neutrality
			    }
			    create_country_leader = {
				    name = "Alessandro Pirzio Biroli"
